// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\ApplicationBootstrapper.cs
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Factories;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Modules;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using LoggerFactory = LeadsManagerCORE.Factories.LoggerFactory;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE
{

    public class ApplicationBootstrapper
    {
        private AppSettings _settings;
        private ILogger _logger;

        public ApplicationBootstrapper()
        {
            _logger = LoggerFactory.CreateLogger("Main");
            _settings = LoadConfiguration();
            ValidateSettings(_settings);
            InitializeGlobals(_settings);
        }

        public ICommand? ResolveCommand(string[] args)
        {
            return CommandFactory.GetCommand(args[0], _settings);
        }

        private AppSettings LoadConfiguration()
        {
            try
            {
                var builder = new ConfigurationBuilder()
                .SetBasePath(AppContext.BaseDirectory)
                .AddJsonFile("appsettings.json", optional: false, reloadOnChange: true);

                var config = builder.Build();
                var settings = new AppSettings();
                config.Bind(settings);
                return settings;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                _logger.LogError(ex, "Error loading configuration");
                throw;
            }
        }

        private void ValidateSettings(AppSettings settings)
        {
            if (settings.Dropbox == null ||
            string.IsNullOrEmpty(settings.Dropbox.AppKey) ||
            string.IsNullOrEmpty(settings.Dropbox.AppSecret) ||
            string.IsNullOrEmpty(settings.Dropbox.RefreshToken))
            {
                throw new InvalidOperationException("Dropbox settings are not properly configured.");
            }
        }

        private void InitializeGlobals(AppSettings settings)
        {
            Global.ExcelDownloadPath = Path.Combine(settings.OhioCrash.ExcelDownloadPath, DateTime.Today.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"));
            Global.ExcelFilePath = Path.Combine(settings.ExcelOutputPath, $"FilteredReports_{DateTime.Now:yyyyMMdd}.xlsx");
        }
    }

}

// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Program.cs
/*
 * Leads Manager CORE
 * 29 April 2025
 * Jacob Hayes
 * Purpose: Run automated processes to manage leads in the Bankruptcy and Personal Injury spheres.
 * The scraper will put items into the databases, and this program will manage those leads by:
 * 
 * 
 * BANKRUPTCY WORKFLOW:
 * - Uploading the leads to LeadDocket for future follow-up
 * - Uploading the leads to SkipTrace to obtain phone numbers
 * - Downloading the previous day's results from SkipTrace
 * - Inserting the results into the database
 * 
 * PERSONAL INJURY WORKFLOW:
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * To use this program:
 * Command line arguments must be provided for the program to run.
 * Use --help to see the available options.
 * 1: Run BKWorkflow
 * 2: Run PIWorkflow
 */

/*
 * Helper Class Explanations:
 * AppSettings.cs reads AppSettings.json and binds the values to a class.
 * IOHelper.cs handles input and output file operations.
 * LeadDocketHelper.cs handles the LeadDocket API calls.
 * SeleniumHelper.cs (nonstatic) handles the Selenium WebDriver operations.
 * SkipTraceHelper.cs handles the SkipTrace web interface operations.
 * SqlHelper.cs handles the SQL database operations.
 */

using System;
using System.Net;
using Microsoft.Data.SqlClient;
using Microsoft.IdentityModel.Tokens;
using OpenQA.Selenium; // for web scraping
using OpenQA.Selenium.Chrome;
using NLog; // for logging
using OpenQA.Selenium.Support.UI;
using SeleniumExtras;
using static System.Runtime.InteropServices.JavaScript.JSType;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using System.Data;
using WebDriverManager;
using WebDriverManager.DriverConfigs.Impl;
using WebDriverManager.Helpers;
using LeadsManagerCORE;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Workflows;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Factories;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Modules;
using System.Diagnostics;
using AmourgisCOREServices;

partial class Program
{
    //public static bool debug = true;
    public static IConfiguration Configuration { get; private set; }

    static async Task Main(string[] args)
    {
        // Don't run if there's nothing TO run
        if (args.Length == 0)
        {
            Console.WriteLine("Please provide a command argument.");
            return;
        }

        // Let the Bootstrapper handle setup
        var app = new ApplicationBootstrapper();

        // Let the Bootstrapper resolve the command
        var command = app.ResolveCommand(args);

        // If the command is null, it means the command was not found
        if (command == null)
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"Invalid command: {args[0]}");
            return;
        }

        // Execute the ICommand's ExecuteAsync method and pass it command-line arguments so it can run more granularly.
        await command.ExecuteAsync(args);


    }
}

// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Factories\CommandFactory.cs
/* CommandFactory
 * Jake Hayes
 * 2025 May 15
 * Purpose: Build the workflows
*/
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Modules;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Workflows;
using AmourgisCOREServices;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Factories
{

    public static class CommandFactory
    {
        public static ICommand? GetCommand(string key, AppSettings settings)
        {
            return key switch
            {
                "1" => new BKWorkflow(settings, new AMO_Logger("BKWorkflow")),
                "2" => new PIRapidMailDispatch(settings, new AMO_Logger("PIRapidMailDispatch")),
                "3" => new OhioCrashFetch(settings, new AMO_Logger("OhioCrashFetch")),
                "4" => new PrintLocalLetters(settings, new AMO_Logger("PrintLocalLetters")),
                "D1" => new GetManifestResourceNames(),
                // _ in key switch is equivalent to default in switch(case)
                _ => null
            };
        }
    }

}

// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Modules\DropboxHelper.cs
/*
 * DropboxHelper
 * Jacob Hayes
 * May 2025
 * 
 * I asked GitHub Copilot about the practice of instantiating a new DropboxClient each time we need to use it, and it said:

Keep your current pattern unless you see a measurable performance issue.
•	If you want to optimize, you can:
•	Store a single DropboxClient as a private field.
•	On token refresh, dispose and recreate the client.
•	Wrap all Dropbox API calls in retry logic that can handle token expiration (and refresh/recreate as needed).
•	For batch/utility apps: new DropboxClient per operation is fine and avoids token issues.
•	For long-running apps: reuse DropboxClient, but recreate it after token refresh.
•	Always ensure you use a valid, non-expired access token for each client.

 * So this is fine for now.
 */



using Dropbox.Api.Files;
using Dropbox.Api;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using System.Text.Json;
using NLog;
using System.Text.Json.Serialization;
using AmourgisCOREServices;
using DocumentFormat.OpenXml.Drawing;
using Org.BouncyCastle.Pqc.Crypto.Lms;
using static Dropbox.Api.Sharing.ListFileMembersIndividualResult;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Modules
{
    internal class DropboxHelper : IDropboxHelper
    {
        private readonly string _clientId;
        private readonly string _clientSecret;
        private readonly string _refreshToken;
        private string _accessToken;
        private AMO_Logger logger;

        public DropboxHelper(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            _clientId = appSettings.Dropbox.AppKey;
            _clientSecret = appSettings.Dropbox.AppSecret;
            _refreshToken = appSettings.Dropbox.RefreshToken;
            this.logger = logger;

            logger.Info("Initializing DropboxHelper...");
            // Generate a new access token using the refresh token
            RefreshAccessTokenAsync().Wait();
        }


        private async Task<(TResult result, int attempts)> RetryAsync<TResult>(Func<Task<TResult>> action, int maxRetries = 5, int delayMs = 1000)
        {
            int attempt = 0;
            Exception lastException = null; // Store the last exception to throw it later if needed

            while (true)
            {

                attempt++;
                try
                {
                    //logger.Info($"Attempting action... Attempt {attempt + 1} of {maxRetries}.");
                    return (await action(), attempt);
                }
                catch (Dropbox.Api.RetryException ex) // Transient Dropbox error
                {
                    lastException = ex;
                    logger.Error($"Transient Dropbox error: {ex.Message}. Attempt {attempt} of {maxRetries}.");
                }
                catch (Exception ex) // Network error
                {
                    lastException = ex;
                    logger.Error(ex, $"Error: {ex.Message}. Attempt {attempt} of {maxRetries}.");
                }
                // Add more catch blocks for other transient errors if needed



                // Now we can throw the last exception explicitly
                throw lastException ?? new Exception("Unknown error occurred during retry.");



                // Wait longer for rate limit (exponential backoff)
                await Task.Delay(delayMs * (int)Math.Pow(2, attempt)); // Exponential backoff
            }
        }


        public async Task RefreshAccessTokenAsync()
        {
            // Ask Dropbox for a token using the refresh_token, app_key, and app_secret
            try
            {
                using (var client = new HttpClient())
                {
                    var request = new HttpRequestMessage(HttpMethod.Post, "https://api.dropboxapi.com/oauth2/token");
                    var content = new FormUrlEncodedContent(new[]
                    {
                new KeyValuePair<string, string>("grant_type", "refresh_token"),
                new KeyValuePair<string, string>("refresh_token", _refreshToken),
                new KeyValuePair<string, string>("client_id", _clientId),
                new KeyValuePair<string, string>("client_secret", _clientSecret)
            });
                    request.Content = content;

                    var response = await client.SendAsync(request);

                    // Log the full response body for debugging
                    var responseBody = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                    if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                    {
                        logger.Error($"Dropbox API Error: {responseBody}");
                        response.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
                    }

                    var tokenResponse = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<DropboxTokenResponse>(responseBody);

                    _accessToken = tokenResponse.AccessToken;

                    // Optionally, save the new access token to a secure location
                    logger.Info("Access token refreshed successfully.");
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error($"Error refreshing access token: {ex.Message}");
                throw;
            }
            }

        public string GetAccessToken()
        {
            return _accessToken;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Uploads a file to Dropbox.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="localFilePath">The full local file path</param>
        /// <param name="dropboxFolderPath">The relative dropbox file path</param>
        /// <returns></returns>
        public async Task UploadFileAsync(string localFilePath, string dropboxFolderPath)
        {
            await RetryAsync(
                async () =>
                {
                    try
                    {
                        using (var dbx = new DropboxClient(_accessToken))
                        {
                            using (var fileStream = File.OpenRead(localFilePath))
                            {
                                string dropboxFilePath = $"{dropboxFolderPath}/{System.IO.Path.GetFileName(localFilePath)}";
                                await dbx.Files.UploadAsync(dropboxFilePath, WriteMode.Overwrite.Instance, body: fileStream);
                                logger.Info($"File {localFilePath} uploaded to Dropbox at {dropboxFilePath}");
                                return true;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    catch (Exception ex)
                    {
                        logger.Error($"Error uploading file to Dropbox: {ex.Message}");
                        throw;
                    }
                }
            );
        }


        public async Task DownloadFileFromDropboxAsync(string dropboxFilePath, string localFilePath)
        {
            var (success, attemptsUsed) = await RetryAsync(
                async () =>
                {
                    try
                    {
                        // NB that each using creates a new block, it just looks nice this way. If you need to make changes, add the brackets {} so that the using blocks are clear.
                        using (var dbx = new DropboxClient(_accessToken))
                        using (var response = await dbx.Files.DownloadAsync(dropboxFilePath))
                        using (var contentStream = await response.GetContentAsStreamAsync())
                        using (var fileStream = File.Create(localFilePath))
                        {
                            await contentStream.CopyToAsync(fileStream);
                            
                        }
                    }
                    catch (Exception ex)
                    {
                        logger.Error($"Error downloading file from Dropbox: {ex.Message}");
                        throw;
                    }

                    return true;
                }
            );

            logger.Info($"Attempt {attemptsUsed} success: File {dropboxFilePath} downloaded from Dropbox to {localFilePath}");
        }


        public async Task<bool> DeleteFileFromDropboxAsync(string dropboxFilePath)
        {
            // Check if the file path is null or empty
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(dropboxFilePath))
            {
                logger.Warn("Dropbox file path is null or empty.");
                return true;
            }

            var (result, attemptsUsed) = await RetryAsync(
                async () =>
                {
                    try
                    {
                        using (var dbx = new DropboxClient(_accessToken))
                        {
                            await dbx.Files.DeleteV2Async(dropboxFilePath);
                            return true;
                        }
                    }
                    catch (Exception ex)
                    {
                        logger.Error($"Error deleting file from Dropbox: {ex.Message}");
                        return false;
                    }
                }
            );

            logger.Info($"File {dropboxFilePath} deleted from Dropbox on attempt number {attemptsUsed}");
            return result;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Checks if a file exists in Dropbox.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="path"></param>
        /// <returns>True if the file exists, false otherwise</returns>
        public async Task<bool> FileExistsInDropboxAsync(string path)
        {
            using (var dbx = new DropboxClient(_accessToken))
            {
                try
                {
                    var metadata = await dbx.Files.GetMetadataAsync(path);
                    return metadata.IsFile;
                }
                catch (ApiException<GetMetadataError>) // Metadata error means the file was not found, so false
                {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }



        /// <summary>
        /// Moves a file from one location to another in Dropbox.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="fileNames"></param>
        /// <param name="sourceFolderPath"></param>
        /// <param name="destinationFolderPath"></param>
        /// <returns></returns>
        public async Task<List<string>> MoveFilesAsync(List<string> fileNames, string sourceFolderPath, string destinationFolderPath)
        {
            List<string> movedFiles = new List<string>();

            using (var dbx = new DropboxClient(_accessToken))
            {
                foreach (var fileName in fileNames)
                {
                    string sourcePath = $"{sourceFolderPath}/{fileName}";
                    string destinationPath = $"{destinationFolderPath}/{fileName}";

                    var (result, attempts) = await RetryAsync(
                        async () =>
                        {
                            try
                            {
                                await dbx.Files.MoveV2Async(sourcePath, destinationPath);
                            }
                            catch (ApiException<RelocationError>)
                            {
                                logger.Info($"{fileName} not found, skipping... ");
                                return true; // Return early to skip retries
                            }
                            return true;
                        }
                    );
                    if (result)
                    {
                        logger.Info($"Moved file {fileName} from {sourcePath} to {destinationPath}");
                        movedFiles.Add(fileName);
                    }
                }
            }
        
            return movedFiles;
        }


        // TODO: either add retryAfter logic OR delete the folder and remake it, whichever is smoother.
        public async Task ClearFolderAsync(string folderPath)
        {
            using (var dbx = new DropboxClient(_accessToken, 
                new DropboxClientConfig {
                    HttpClient = new HttpClient { Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(2) } 
                }))
            {
                var listFolderResult = await dbx.Files.ListFolderAsync(folderPath);

                foreach (var item in listFolderResult.Entries)
                {
                    // wait to try to avoid too many requests
                    Thread.Sleep(500);

                    // try up to 3 times per item to delete
                    int retryCount = 3;
                    for (int i = 0; i < retryCount; i++)
                    {
                        try
                        {
                            await dbx.Files.DeleteV2Async(item.PathLower);
                            logger.Info($"Deleted file {item.Name} from {folderPath}");
                            break; // Exit loop if request is successful
                        }
                        catch (ApiException<RelocationError> ex)
                        {
                            logger.Error($"Error deleting file {item.Name}: {ex.Message}");
                            if (i == retryCount - 1)
                            {
                                throw; // Rethrow exception if all retries fail
                            }
                        }
                        catch (HttpRequestException ex)
                        {
                            logger.Error($"Request failed: {ex.Message}");
                            if (i == retryCount - 1)
                            {
                                throw; // Rethrow exception if all retries fail
                            }
                        }
                    }

                }
            }
        }

    }


    public class DropboxTokenResponse
    {
        [JsonPropertyName("access_token")]
        public string AccessToken { get; set; }

        [JsonPropertyName("token_type")]
        public string TokenType { get; set; }

        [JsonPropertyName("expires_in")]
        public int ExpiresIn { get; set; }
    }

}


// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Modules\IOHelper.cs
using Microsoft.Data.SqlClient;
using NLog;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using System.Data;
using ExcelDataReader; // To read Excel files
using NPOI.SS.UserModel; // For writing Excel files
using NPOI.XSSF.UserModel;
using AmourgisCOREServices;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Modules
{
    internal class IOHelper : IIOHelper
    {
        private readonly AppSettings appSettings;
        private readonly AMO_Logger logger;
        private static readonly int MaxRecordsPerFile = 100; // Maximum number of records per split file

        public IOHelper(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            this.appSettings = appSettings;
            this.logger = logger;
        }


        /// <summary>
        /// Deletes a file if it exists. Returns true if it was deleted or didn't exist, false if an error occurred.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="filePath">The full Path of the file</param>
        /// <returns>True if it was deleted or didn't exist, false if an error occurred.</returns>
        public bool DeleteFileIfExists(string filePath)
        {
            if (File.Exists(filePath))
            {
                try
                {
                    File.Delete(filePath);
                    logger.Info($"File {filePath} deleted successfully.");
                    return true;
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    logger.Error($"Error deleting file {filePath}: {ex.Message}");
                    return false;
                }
            }
            else
            {
                logger.Warn($"File {filePath} does not exist.");
                return true;
            }
        }


        public DataTable ExcelToDataTable(string excelFilePath)
        {
            if (!File.Exists(excelFilePath))
            {
                logger.Error($"The file {excelFilePath} does not exist.");
                throw new FileNotFoundException($"The file {excelFilePath} does not exist.");
            }

            // Ensure the ExcelDataReader library can read the file
            System.Text.Encoding.RegisterProvider(System.Text.CodePagesEncodingProvider.Instance);

            using (var stream = File.Open(excelFilePath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read))
            {
                using (var reader = ExcelReaderFactory.CreateReader(stream))
                {
                    // Use the AsDataSet method to load the Excel file into a DataSet
                    var result = reader.AsDataSet(new ExcelDataSetConfiguration
                    {
                        ConfigureDataTable = _ => new ExcelDataTableConfiguration
                        {
                            UseHeaderRow = true // Skip the header row
                        }
                    });

                    // Return the first DataTable (assuming the Excel file has only one sheet)
                    return result.Tables[0];
                }
            }
        }

        public static void ExportComprehensiveToCSV(SqlDataReader reader, string saveLocation, DateTime queryStartDate, bool includeHeader = true)
        {
            Directory.CreateDirectory(saveLocation);
            var comprehensiveFilePath = $@"{saveLocation}{queryStartDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")}_comprehensive.csv";

            using (var writer = new StreamWriter(comprehensiveFilePath))
            {

                if (includeHeader) WriteHeaderRow(writer);


                while (reader.Read())
                {
                    WriteRecordRow(reader, writer);
                }
            }
        }

        private static void WriteHeaderRow(StreamWriter writer)
        {
            writer.Write("Report Number, First Name, Last Name, Street Address, City, State, Zip, Country, Date of Birth");
            writer.WriteLine();
        }

        private static void WriteRecordRow(SqlDataReader reader, StreamWriter writer)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i < reader.FieldCount; i++)
            {
                writer.Write(reader[i].ToString());
                if (i < reader.FieldCount - 1)
                {
                    writer.Write(",");
                }
            }
            writer.WriteLine();
        }


        public static int SplitCsvFile(DateTime queryStartDate, string sourceFilePath, string destinationFolderPath, bool includeHeader = true)
        {
            Directory.CreateDirectory(destinationFolderPath); // Ensure the folder exists

            int fileCount = 1;
            using (var reader = new StreamReader(sourceFilePath))
            {
                string headerLine = includeHeader ? reader.ReadLine() : null;
                int recordCount = 0;

                var splitFilePath = Path.Combine(destinationFolderPath, $"{queryStartDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")}_split_file_{fileCount}.csv");
                var writer = new StreamWriter(splitFilePath);

                if (includeHeader && headerLine != null)
                {
                    var headers = headerLine.Split(',');
                    writer.WriteLine(string.Join(",", headers.Take(9)));
                }

                while (!reader.EndOfStream)
                {
                    if (recordCount >= MaxRecordsPerFile)
                    {
                        writer.Close();
                        fileCount++;
                        recordCount = 0;
                        splitFilePath = Path.Combine(destinationFolderPath, $"{queryStartDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")}_split_file_{fileCount}.csv");
                        writer = new StreamWriter(splitFilePath);

                        if (includeHeader && headerLine != null)
                        {
                            var headers = headerLine.Split(',');
                            writer.WriteLine(string.Join(",", headers.Take(9)));
                        }
                    }

                    string? line = reader.ReadLine();
                    var columns = line.Split(',');
                    writer.WriteLine(string.Join(",", columns.Take(9)));
                    recordCount++;
                }

                writer.Close();
            }

            return fileCount;
        }

        internal void DataTableToExcel(DataTable records, string excelFilePath)
        {
            if (records == null || records.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                throw new ArgumentException("The DataTable is empty or null.");
            }


            // Ensure all directories in the path to excelFilePath are created
            string directoryPath = Path.GetDirectoryName(excelFilePath);
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(directoryPath))
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(directoryPath);
            }


            // Create a new workbook and a sheet
            IWorkbook workbook = new XSSFWorkbook();
            ISheet sheet = workbook.CreateSheet("FilteredReports");

            // Create the header row
            IRow headerRow = sheet.CreateRow(0);
            for (int i = 0; i < records.Columns.Count; i++)
            {
                headerRow.CreateCell(i).SetCellValue(records.Columns[i].ColumnName);
            }

            // Populate the data rows
            for (int i = 0; i < records.Rows.Count; i++)
            {
                IRow dataRow = sheet.CreateRow(i + 1); // Start from row 1 (row 0 is the header)
                for (int j = 0; j < records.Columns.Count; j++)
                {
                    dataRow.CreateCell(j).SetCellValue(records.Rows[i][j]?.ToString() ?? string.Empty);
                }
            }

            // Auto-size all columns for better readability
            for (int i = 0; i < records.Columns.Count; i++)
            {
                sheet.AutoSizeColumn(i);
            }

            // Save the workbook to the specified file path
            using (var fileStream = new FileStream(excelFilePath, FileMode.Create, FileAccess.Write))
            {
                workbook.Write(fileStream);
            }

            Console.WriteLine($"Excel file successfully created at {excelFilePath}");
        }

    }
}

        private async Task<bool> AddRecordToLeadDocketAsync(Dictionary<string, string> leadData)
        {
            try
            {
                using (HttpClient client = new HttpClient())
                {

                    var jsonContent = new StringContent(JsonConvert.SerializeObject(leadData), Encoding.UTF8, "application/json");

                    HttpResponseMessage response = await client.PostAsync("https://amourgis.leaddocket.com/opportunities/formjson/8", jsonContent);
                    response.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
                    logger.Info($"Sent lead data to LeadDocket: {JsonConvert.SerializeObject(leadData)} with response {await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync()}");

                    return true;
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error($"An error occurred while trying to add record to LeadDocket: {ex.Message}");
                return false;
            }
        }
    }
}

// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Modules\PrintHelper.cs
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Data;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using AmourgisCOREServices;
using DocumentFormat.OpenXml.Packaging;
using DocumentFormat.OpenXml.Wordprocessing;
using OpenQA.Selenium;
using Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word;
using DocumentFormat.OpenXml.ExtendedProperties;
using System.Diagnostics;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Modules
{
    internal class PrintHelper
    {
        private AppSettings appSettings;
        private AMO_Logger logger;
        private PdfPrinter pdfPrinter;

        public PrintHelper(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            // Initialize the PrintHelper with the provided AppSettings
            this.appSettings = appSettings;
            this.logger = logger;
            this.pdfPrinter = new PdfPrinter(appSettings, logger);
        }




        /// <summary>
        /// Generates a filled document based on a template and data from a DataRow.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="templatePath"></param>
        /// <param name="outputPath"></param>
        /// <param name="data"></param>
        /// <returns></returns>
        public string GenerateFilledDocument(string templatePath, string outputPath, DataRow data)
        {
            File.Copy(templatePath, outputPath, overwrite: true); // Step 1: Copy template to output path
            FillContentControls(outputPath, data);      // Step 2: Fill
            return outputPath;                         // Step 3: Return path to the filled doc
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Fills the content controls in a Word document with data from a DataRow.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="wordFilePath"></param>
        /// <param name="data"></param>
        private void FillContentControls(string wordFilePath, DataRow data)
        {
            using (WordprocessingDocument wordDoc = WordprocessingDocument.Open(wordFilePath, true))
            {
                // Fill content controls with data
                var sdtElements = wordDoc.MainDocumentPart.Document.Descendants<SdtElement>();

                // Loop through each content control and fill it with data
                foreach (SdtElement sdt in sdtElements)
                {
                    var tag = sdt.SdtProperties.GetFirstChild<Tag>()?.Val.Value;
                    if (tag != null && data.Table.Columns.Contains(tag))
                    {
                        var text = sdt.Descendants<Text>().FirstOrDefault();
                        if (text != null)
                            text.Text = data[tag].ToString();
                    }
                }
                wordDoc.MainDocumentPart.Document.Save();
            }
        }

        public string ConvertToPdf(string docxPath, string pdfPath = null)
        {
            if (pdfPath == null)
                pdfPath = Path.ChangeExtension(docxPath, ".pdf");

            var wordApp = new Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.Application();
            try
            {
                wordApp.Visible = false;
                wordApp.DisplayAlerts = WdAlertLevel.wdAlertsNone;

                var doc = wordApp.Documents.Open(docxPath, ReadOnly: true, Visible: false);
                doc.ExportAsFixedFormat(
                    pdfPath,
                    WdExportFormat.wdExportFormatPDF,
                    OpenAfterExport: false,
                    OptimizeFor: WdExportOptimizeFor.wdExportOptimizeForPrint,
                    Range: WdExportRange.wdExportAllDocument,
                    Item: WdExportItem.wdExportDocumentContent,
                    IncludeDocProps: true,
                    KeepIRM: true,
                    CreateBookmarks: WdExportCreateBookmarks.wdExportCreateWordBookmarks,
                    DocStructureTags: true,
                    BitmapMissingFonts: true,
                    UseISO19005_1: false
                );
                doc.Close(false);
                return pdfPath;
            }
            finally
            {
                wordApp.Quit();
            }
        }


        public void PrintWordDocument(string docxPath, string printerName = null)
        {
            printerName = string.IsNullOrEmpty(printerName) ? appSettings.Printer.ColorPrinter : printerName;

            var wordApp = new Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.Application();
            try
            {
                wordApp.Visible = false;
                wordApp.DisplayAlerts = WdAlertLevel.wdAlertsNone;




                var doc = wordApp.Documents.Open(docxPath, ReadOnly: true, Visible: false);


                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(printerName))
                {
                    wordApp.ActivePrinter = printerName;
                }
                logger.LogInformation($"Attempting to print document: {docxPath} on printer: {wordApp.ActivePrinter.ToString()}");
                // Allow the Word application to be visible to ensure window context, then hide after printing
                wordApp.Visible = true;
                // Activate the document to ensure it is in focus
                doc.Activate();
                doc.PrintOut(Background: false);
                wordApp.Visible = false;
                doc.Close(false);
            }
            finally
            {
                wordApp.Quit();
            }

        }

        public void PrintPDFDocument(string pdfPath, string printerName = null, bool duplex = true, IEnumerable<int> pages = null)
        {
            Thread.Sleep(1000); // Wait for 1 second to ensure the printer is ready

            printerName = string.IsNullOrEmpty(printerName) ? appSettings.Printer.ColorPrinter : printerName;
                        
            pdfPrinter.PrintPdf(pdfPath, printerName, duplex, pages);

        }



        private class PdfPrinter
        {
            private readonly AppSettings appSettings;
            private readonly AMO_Logger logger;

            public PdfPrinter(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
            {
                this.appSettings = appSettings;
                this.logger = logger;
            }

            public void PrintPdf(string pdfPath, string printerName, bool duplex = true, IEnumerable<int> pages = null)
            {
                string sumatraPath = appSettings.Sumatra.ExecutablePath;
                string duplexSetting = duplex ? "duplexlong" : "simplex";

                // Choose the list of pages to print
                string pageList = pages != null && pages.Any()
                 ? string.Join(",", pages)
                 : "";

                string printSettings = string.IsNullOrEmpty(pageList)
                ? duplexSetting
                : $"{pageList},{duplexSetting}";

                var psi = new ProcessStartInfo
                {
                    FileName = sumatraPath,
                    Arguments = $"-print-to \"{printerName}\" -print-settings \"{printSettings}\" -exit-when-done \"{pdfPath}\"",
                    CreateNoWindow = true,
                    UseShellExecute = false
                };

                try
                {
                    using var process = Process.Start(psi);
                    process.WaitForExit();
                    logger.Info($"PDF printed successfully to {printerName} with {printSettings}");
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    logger.Error(ex, $"Error printing PDF");
                    throw;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}


// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Modules\SeleniumHelper.cs
/* SeleniumHelper.cs
 * 2025 April 09
 * Jacob Hayes
 * 
 * This class uses WebDriverManager to ensure that it is using the latest version of ChromeDriver.
    Setup and Teardown: Initialize and dispose of the Selenium WebDriver.
    Navigation: Navigate to URLs and handle page interactions.
    Element Interaction: Click buttons, fill forms, and interact with web elements.
    File Download: Handle the download of files from the web.
 */

using OpenQA.Selenium.Chrome;
using OpenQA.Selenium.Support.UI;
using OpenQA.Selenium;
using WebDriverManager;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using WebDriverManager.DriverConfigs.Impl;
using NLog;
using SeleniumExtras.WaitHelpers;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using WebDriverManager.Helpers;
using AmourgisCOREServices;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Modules
{
    // ensure that the class implements IDisposable to clean up resources
    // we don't need to implement another interface here - SeleniumHelper is already a wrapper for a WebDriver and is abstracted enough
    public class SeleniumHelper : IDisposable
    {
        private static AMO_Logger logger;
        private IWebDriver driver;
        private WebDriverWait wait;

        public SeleniumHelper(AMO_Logger alogger, string? downloadPath = null, bool headless = false, bool startMinimized = false)
        {
            logger = alogger;
            // Use WebDriverManager to set up the ChromeDriver
            new DriverManager().SetUpDriver(new ChromeConfig(), VersionResolveStrategy.MatchingBrowser);
            var options = new ChromeOptions();
            if (downloadPath != null)
                options.AddUserProfilePreference("download.default_directory", downloadPath); // to allow for us to customize the download path
            options.AddUserProfilePreference("download.prompt_for_download", false);
            options.AddUserProfilePreference("disable-popup-blocking", true);

            if (headless)
            {
                options.AddArgument("--headless=new"); // 'new' is more stable in recent Chrome versions
                options.AddArgument("--disable-gpu");
                options.AddArgument("--window-size=1920,1080");
            }
            else if (startMinimized)
            {
                options.AddArgument("--start-minimized");
            }


            driver = new ChromeDriver(options);
            wait = new WebDriverWait(driver, TimeSpan.FromMinutes(30));
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// JH: Selenium workaround to select a combobox value.
        /// We needed this because if we tried to click on the text of the dropdown, it would fail to select the value.
        /// By using the down and Enter keys, we can select the value without needing to click on the dropdown.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="labelText">The string of the text of the label of the combobox.</param>
        /// <param name="valueToEnter">The text of the value we want to select.</param>
        public void SelectComboboxValueByLabel(string labelText, string valueToEnter)
        {
            // Find the label element by its text
            IWebElement label = this.wait.Until(SeleniumExtras.WaitHelpers.ExpectedConditions.ElementIsVisible(By.XPath($"//label[text()='{labelText}']")));

            // Find the input element associated with the label
            IWebElement input = label.FindElement(By.XPath("following-sibling::div//input"));

            // Click to focus on the input field
            input.Click();

            // Type the desired value
            input.SendKeys(valueToEnter);

            // Press DOWN arrow key to highlight the option
            input.SendKeys(Keys.ArrowDown);

            // Press ENTER to select the option
            input.SendKeys(Keys.Enter);
        }

        public IWebElement WaitUntilElementIsVisible(By selector)
        {
            try
            {
                return wait.Until(ExpectedConditions.ElementIsVisible(selector));
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, $"Failed to wait for element {selector} to be visible");
                throw;
            }
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            driver.Quit();
            driver.Dispose();
        }



        public void NavigateToUrl(string url)
        {
            try
            {
                driver.Navigate().GoToUrl(url);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, $"Failed to navigate to {url}: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        public void SendKeysToElement(By selector, string keysToSend)
        {
            try
            {
                wait.Until(d => d.FindElement(selector));
                var element = driver.FindElement(selector);
                element.SendKeys(keysToSend);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, $"Failed to send keys to element {selector}");
            }
        }


        public void ClickElement(By selector)
        {
            try
            {
                wait.Until(ExpectedConditions.ElementToBeClickable(selector));
                var element = driver.FindElement(selector);
                element.Click();
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, $"Failed to click element {selector}: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

    }

}

using NLog;
using OpenQA.Selenium.Chrome;
using OpenQA.Selenium.Support.UI;
using OpenQA.Selenium;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using Microsoft.IdentityModel.Tokens;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using AmourgisCOREServices;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Modules
{
    
    public class SkipTraceHelper : ISkipTraceHelper
    {
        private readonly AppSettings appSettings;
        private readonly AMO_Logger logger;

        public SkipTraceHelper(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            this.appSettings = appSettings;
            this.logger = logger;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Navigate to SkipTrace, log in, and download the results for the specified date.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="dtResultDate"></param>
        /// <param name="appSettings"></param>
        public void DownloadSkipTraceResults(DateTime dtResultDate, string downloadPath = "")
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"Downloading SkipTrace results for {dtResultDate.ToShortDateString()}...");
            bool hasFoundAtLeastOneFile = false;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(downloadPath))
                downloadPath = Path.Combine(appSettings.DownloadDirectory, dtResultDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"), "Downloaded from SkipTrace");

            // Create the directory if it doesn't exist (if it does, nothing will happen).
            Directory.CreateDirectory(downloadPath);

            using (SeleniumHelper shDriver = new SeleniumHelper(logger, downloadPath))
            {
                try
                {
                    // Navigate to the SkipTrace login page
                    shDriver.NavigateToUrl(appSettings.SkipTrace.DownloadUrl); // Use the passed-in appSettings object
                    shDriver.SendKeysToElement(By.Name("email"), appSettings.SkipTrace.Username); // Use appSettings for credentials
                    shDriver.SendKeysToElement(By.Name("password"), appSettings.SkipTrace.Password);
                    // Click the login button
                    shDriver.ClickElement(By.CssSelector("button[type='submit']"));


                    // Wait until we can see the files we need to download
                    IWebElement tableBody = shDriver.WaitUntilElementIsVisible(By.ClassName("InovuaReactDataGrid__body"));
                    logger.Info("Logged in to SkipTrace and found Inovua table.");

                    // Locate all rows in the table
                    IList<IWebElement> rows = tableBody.FindElements(By.ClassName("InovuaReactDataGrid__row"));
                    logger.Info($"Found {rows.Count} rows in the table.");

                    string targetDate = dtResultDate.ToString("d MMM, yyyy");

                    foreach (var row in rows)
                    {
                        IWebElement dateCell = row.FindElement(By.CssSelector("[data-props-id='created_at'] .InovuaReactDataGrid__cell__content"));
                        logger.Info($"Found date cell with text: {dateCell.Text}");

                        if (dateCell.Text.Contains(targetDate))
                        {
                            hasFoundAtLeastOneFile = true;

                            IWebElement downloadLink = row.FindElement(By.CssSelector("[data-props-id='csv_file'] .btn-set"));
                            logger.Info("Date is a match. Attempting to download.");

                            downloadLink.Click();
                            System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(5000); // Adjust this as needed
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            logger.Info("Date does not match target date.");
                        }
                    }

                    if (!hasFoundAtLeastOneFile)
                    {
                        logger.Error($"No files found for date: {dtResultDate.ToShortDateString()}");
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        logger.Info($"Files downloaded successfully for date: {dtResultDate.ToShortDateString()}");
                    }
                }

                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    logger.Error(ex, $"Error logging into SkipTrace: {ex.Message}");
                }
            }
        }


        public void UploadLeadsToSkipTrace(DateTime date)
        {
            // Get yesterday's leads from the database

        }

        public void DownloadExcelSheetFromOhioCrash(string url, string downloadPath, int size = 100)
        {
            // Implementation for downloading the Excel sheet using Selenium
            using (SeleniumHelper shDriver = new SeleniumHelper(logger, downloadPath))
            {
                // Navigate and login
                shDriver.NavigateToUrl(url);
                shDriver.WaitUntilElementIsVisible(By.Id("username"));
                shDriver.SendKeysToElement(By.Id("username"), appSettings.OhioCrash.Username);
                shDriver.SendKeysToElement(By.Id("password"), appSettings.OhioCrash.Password);
                shDriver.ClickElement(By.XPath("//input[@type='submit']"));

                // Wait until we can view most recent reports
                shDriver.WaitUntilElementIsVisible(By.LinkText("View Most Recent Reports"));
                //shDriver.ClickElement(By.LinkText("View Most Recent Reports"));

                // Instead of clicking it, navigate to a special URL to get ALL of the daily reports:
                shDriver.NavigateToUrl($"https://www.ohiocrash.com/search/recent/active?" +
                    $"startDate={DateTime.Today.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")}" +
                    $"&endDate={DateTime.Today.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")}" +
                    $"&size={size}&page=0");

                // Select all and download Excel sheet
                shDriver.WaitUntilElementIsVisible(By.ClassName("select-all"));
                shDriver.ClickElement(By.ClassName("select-all"));
                shDriver.ClickElement(By.Id("download-report-button"));

                Thread.Sleep(5000); // Wait for the download to complete


            }
        }
    }

// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Modules\SqlHelper.cs
using Microsoft.Data.SqlClient;
using NLog;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Data;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using ExcelDataReader;
using AmourgisCOREServices;
using System.Reflection;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Modules
{
    public class SqlHelper : ISqlHelper
    {
        private AppSettings appSettings;
        private AMO_Logger logger;

        private readonly string _connectionString;
        private static readonly Dictionary<int, string> ColumnMapping = new Dictionary<int, string>
            {
                {  0, "ReportID" },
                {  1, "CrashSeverity" },
                {  2, "AtFaultDamage" },
                {  3, "ReportingAgency" },
                {  4, "County" },
                {  5, "CrashDate" },
                {  6, "AtFaultOwnerLastName" },
                {  7, "AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle" },
                {  8, "AtFaultUnitNumber" },
                {  9, "AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear" },
                { 10, "AtFaultPolicyNumber" },
                { 11, "VictimLastName" },
                { 12, "VictimFirstMiddle" },
                { 13, "VictimUnitNumber" },
                { 14, "VictimStreetAddress" },
                { 15, "VictimCity" },
                { 16, "VictimStateCode" },
                { 17, "VictimZip" },
                { 18, "VictimPhone" },
                { 19, "VictimBirthdate" },
                { 20, "VictimAge" },
                { 21, "VictimGender" },
                { 22, "VictimInjuries" },
                { 23, "VictimDamage" },
                { 24, "VictimInsurance" },
                { 25, "ReportingNCIC" },
                { 26, "PDFFileName" }
            };

        #region constructors
        // Default constructor uses the connection string from AppSettings
        public SqlHelper(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            if (appSettings?.Sql?.ConnectionString == null)
            {
                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(appSettings.Sql.ConnectionString), "Connection string cannot be null.");
            }

            _connectionString = appSettings.Sql.ConnectionString;
            this.logger = logger;
        }

        // Overloaded constructor allows for a custom connection string
        public SqlHelper(string connectionString, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(connectionString))
            {
                throw new ArgumentException("Connection string cannot be null or empty.", nameof(connectionString));
            }

            _connectionString = connectionString;
            this.logger = logger;
        }
        #endregion



        public static string LoadEmbeddedSql(string resourceName)
        {
            var assembly = Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly();
            using var stream = assembly.GetManifestResourceStream(resourceName);
            using var reader = new StreamReader(stream);
            return reader.ReadToEnd();
        }




        /// <summary>
        /// Inserts crash reports into the SQL database from an xlsx file path.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="excelFilePath">The full path to the file</param>
        public void InsertCrashReportsIntoSqlDatabase(string excelFilePath)
        {
            if (!File.Exists(excelFilePath))
            {
                throw new FileNotFoundException($"The file {excelFilePath} does not exist.");
            }

            System.Text.Encoding.RegisterProvider(System.Text.CodePagesEncodingProvider.Instance);

            using (var stream = File.Open(excelFilePath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read))
            {
                using (var reader = ExcelReaderFactory.CreateReader(stream))
                {
                    using (var connection = new SqlConnection(_connectionString))
                    {
                        connection.Open();

                        while (reader.Read()) // Read each row
                        {
                            // Skip the header row
                            if (reader.Depth == 0) continue;

                            // Build the SQL INSERT command
                            var command = new SqlCommand(
"""
MERGE INTO PersonalInjury.CrashReports AS Target
USING (VALUES (@ReportID, @CrashSeverity, @AtFaultDamage, @ReportingAgency, @County, @CrashDate, @AtFaultOwnerLastName, @AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle, @AtFaultUnitNumber, @AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear, @AtFaultPolicyNumber, @VictimLastName, @VictimFirstMiddle, @VictimUnitNumber, @VictimStreetAddress, @VictimCity, @VictimStateCode, @VictimZip, @VictimPhone, @VictimBirthdate, @VictimAge, @VictimGender, @VictimInjuries, @VictimDamage, @VictimInsurance, @ReportingNCIC, @PDFFileName))
AS Source (ReportID, CrashSeverity, AtFaultDamage, ReportingAgency, County, CrashDate, AtFaultOwnerLastName, AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle, AtFaultUnitNumber, AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear, AtFaultPolicyNumber, VictimLastName, VictimFirstMiddle, VictimUnitNumber, VictimStreetAddress, VictimCity, VictimStateCode, VictimZip, VictimPhone, VictimBirthdate, VictimAge, VictimGender, VictimInjuries, VictimDamage, VictimInsurance, ReportingNCIC, PDFFileName)
ON Target.ReportID = Source.ReportID
   AND Target.VictimFirstMiddle = Source.VictimFirstMiddle
   AND Target.VictimLastName = Source.VictimLastName
WHEN NOT MATCHED BY TARGET THEN
    INSERT (ReportID, CrashSeverity, AtFaultDamage, ReportingAgency, County, CrashDate, AtFaultOwnerLastName, AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle, AtFaultUnitNumber, AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear, AtFaultPolicyNumber, VictimLastName, VictimFirstMiddle, VictimUnitNumber, VictimStreetAddress, VictimCity, VictimStateCode, VictimZip, VictimPhone, VictimBirthdate, VictimAge, VictimGender, VictimInjuries, VictimDamage, VictimInsurance, ReportingNCIC, PDFFileName, CreateTime)
    VALUES (Source.ReportID, Source.CrashSeverity, Source.AtFaultDamage, Source.ReportingAgency, Source.County, Source.CrashDate, Source.AtFaultOwnerLastName, Source.AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle, Source.AtFaultUnitNumber, Source.AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear, Source.AtFaultPolicyNumber, Source.VictimLastName, Source.VictimFirstMiddle, Source.VictimUnitNumber, Source.VictimStreetAddress, Source.VictimCity, Source.VictimStateCode, Source.VictimZip, Source.VictimPhone, Source.VictimBirthdate, Source.VictimAge, Source.VictimGender, Source.VictimInjuries, Source.VictimDamage, Source.VictimInsurance, Source.ReportingNCIC, Source.PDFFileName, GETDATE());
"""
                                , connection);
                                

                            // Map each column to its corresponding SQL parameter
                            foreach (var mapping in ColumnMapping)
                            {
                                var columnIndex = mapping.Key;
                                var columnName = mapping.Value;

                                // Add the parameter to the SQL command
                                command.Parameters.AddWithValue($"@{columnName}", reader.GetValue(columnIndex) ?? DBNull.Value);
                            }

                            // Execute the command
                            command.ExecuteNonQuery();
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets filtered reports from 16:00 yesterday to 14:00 today.
        /// </summary>
        /// <returns></returns>
        public DataTable GetFilteredCrashReports()
        {
            DataTable filteredReports = new DataTable();
            try
            {
                using (SqlConnection conn = new SqlConnection(_connectionString))
                {
                    conn.Open();
                    string queryFilterCrashReports =
    // Query to filter crash reports based on specific criteria
    // CreateTime: Between 16:00 yesterday and 14:00 today
    // CAST(CAST(GETDATE() AS DATE) AS DATETIME) gets you today at 00:00
    // CAST(CAST(GETDATE() AS DATE) - 1 AS DATETIME) gets you yesterday at 00:00
    // AtFaultUnitNumber not equal to '98' or '99' (unknown or animal)
    """
SELECT 

ReportID as [Report Number:],
CrashSeverity as [Crash Severity:],
AtFaultDamage as [At Fault Damage:],
ReportingAgency as [Reporting Agency:],
County as [County:],
CrashDate as [Crash Date:],
AtFaultOwnerLastName as [At-Fault Owner Last Name:],
AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle as [At-Fault Owner First Middle:],
AtFaultUnitNumber as [Unit #:],
AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear as [At-Fault Ins. or Car Year:],
AtFaultPolicyNumber as [Policy Number:],
VictimLastName as [Victim's Last Name:],
VictimFirstMiddle as [Victim's First Middle:],
VictimUnitNumber as [Unit #:],
VictimStreetAddress as [Address:],
VictimCity as [City:],
VictimStateCode as [State:],
VictimZip as [Zip:],
VictimPhone as [Phone:],
VictimBirthdate as [Birthdate:],
VictimAge as [Age:],
VictimGender as [Gender:],
VictimInjuries as [Injuries:],
VictimDamage as [Damage:],
VictimInsurance as [Insurance:],
ReportingNCIC as [Reporting NCIC:],
PDFFileName as [File Name:]

FROM PersonalInjury.CrashReports



WHERE CreateTime >= DATEADD(HOUR, 16, DATEADD(DAY, -1, CAST(GETDATE() AS DATETIME)))
AND CreateTime <= DATEADD(HOUR, 14, CAST(CAST(GETDATE() AS DATE) AS DATETIME))


AND AtFaultUnitNumber != '98'
AND AtFaultUnitNumber != '99'
AND AtFaultOwnerLastName NOT LIKE '%Unknown%'
AND VictimLastName IS NOT NULL 
AND TRIM(VictimLastName) != ''
AND VictimFirstMiddle IS NOT NULL
AND TRIM(VictimFirstMiddle) != ''
""";
                    using (SqlCommand cmd = new SqlCommand(queryFilterCrashReports, conn))
                    {
                        using (SqlDataAdapter adapter = new SqlDataAdapter(cmd))
                        {
                            adapter.Fill(filteredReports);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error retrieving filtered crash reports.");
                throw;
            }

            return filteredReports;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets filtered reports from 14:00 to 16:00 today.
        /// </summary>
        /// <returns>A DataTable with data aligned to the form filled sections of the document</returns>
        public DataTable GetLocalFilteredCrashReports(DateTime? targetDate = null)
        {
            // Null coalescing assignment operator to set targetDate to today if null
            targetDate ??= DateTime.Today;

            DataTable filteredReports = new DataTable();
            try
            {
                using (SqlConnection conn = new SqlConnection(_connectionString))
                {
                    conn.Open();
                    string queryFilterCrashReports =
    // Query to filter crash reports based on specific criteria
    // CreateTime: Between 14:00 and 16:00 today
    // CAST(CAST(GETDATE() AS DATE) AS DATETIME) gets you today at 00:00
    // AtFaultUnitNumber not equal to '98' or '99' (unknown or animal)
    """
SELECT

ReportID,
CrashSeverity,
AtFaultDamage,
ReportingAgency,
County,
FORMAT(CrashDate, 'M/d/yyyy') AS CrashDate,
AtFaultOwnerLastName,
AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle,
AtFaultUnitNumber,
AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear,
AtFaultPolicyNumber,
VictimLastName,
VictimFirstMiddle,
VictimUnitNumber,
VictimStreetAddress,
VictimCity,
VictimStateCode,
VictimZip,
VictimPhone,
VictimBirthdate,
VictimAge,
VictimGender,
VictimInjuries,
VictimDamage,
VictimInsurance,
ReportingNCIC,
PDFFileName

FROM PersonalInjury.CrashReports


WHERE CreateTime >= DATEADD(HOUR, 14, @TargetDate)
AND CreateTime <= DATEADD(HOUR, 16, @TargetDate)


AND AtFaultUnitNumber != '98'
AND AtFaultUnitNumber != '99'
AND AtFaultOwnerLastName NOT LIKE '%Unknown%'
AND VictimLastName IS NOT NULL 
AND TRIM(VictimLastName) != ''
AND VictimFirstMiddle IS NOT NULL
AND TRIM(VictimFirstMiddle) != ''

ORDER BY CreateTime DESC
""";
                    using (SqlCommand cmd = new SqlCommand(queryFilterCrashReports, conn))
                    {

                        // Add parameters to the command
                        cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@TargetDate", targetDate.Value.Date);
                        
                        using (SqlDataAdapter adapter = new SqlDataAdapter(cmd))
                        {
                            adapter.Fill(filteredReports);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error retrieving filtered crash reports: " + ex.Message);
                throw;
            }

            return filteredReports;
        }

        public static DataTable GetYesterdaysLeadsFromDatabase(AppSettings appSettings)
        {
            DataTable returnData = new DataTable();
            string connectionString = appSettings.Sql.ConnectionString;
            using (SqlConnection conn = new SqlConnection(connectionString))
            {
                conn.Open();
                string query = "SELECT * FROM AmourgisDB.dbo.YesterdayCases";

                using (SqlCommand cmd = new SqlCommand(query, conn))
                {

                    using (SqlDataAdapter adapter = new SqlDataAdapter(cmd))
                    {
                        adapter.Fill(returnData);
                    }

                }
            }

            return returnData;
        }
    
    
        public DataTable GetPILeadsForLeadDocket(DateTime startDate, DateTime endDate)
        {
            DataTable returnData = new DataTable();
            using (SqlConnection conn = new SqlConnection(_connectionString))
            {
                conn.Open();
                string query = LoadEmbeddedSql("LeadsManagerCORE.sql.queryPILeadsToLeadDocket.sql");
                using (SqlCommand cmd = new SqlCommand(query, conn))
                {
                    cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@StartDate", startDate);
                    cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@EndDate", endDate);
                    using (SqlDataAdapter adapter = new SqlDataAdapter(cmd))
                    {
                        adapter.Fill(returnData);
                    }
                }
            }

            return returnData;
        }
    
    }

// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\sql\queryPILeadsToLeadDocket.sql
-- LeadsManagerCORE.sql.queryPILeadsToLeadDocket.sql

SELECT 

ReportID,
CrashSeverity,
AtFaultDamage,
ReportingAgency,
County,
FORMAT(CrashDate, 'M/d/yyyy') AS CrashDate,
AtFaultOwnerLastName,
AtFaultOwnerFirstMiddle,
AtFaultUnitNumber,
AtFaultInsuranceOrCarYear,
AtFaultPolicyNumber,
VictimLastName,
VictimFirstMiddle,
VictimUnitNumber,
VictimStreetAddress,
VictimCity,
VictimStateCode,
VictimZip,
VictimPhone,
VictimBirthdate,
VictimAge,
VictimGender,
VictimInjuries,
VictimDamage,
VictimInsurance,
ReportingNCIC,
PDFFileName

FROM PersonalInjury.CrashReports


WHERE CreateTime >= @StartDate
-- half-open interval
AND CreateTime < DATEADD(DAY, 1, @EndDate)


AND AtFaultUnitNumber != '98'
AND AtFaultUnitNumber != '99'
AND AtFaultOwnerLastName NOT LIKE '%Unknown%'
AND VictimLastName IS NOT NULL 
AND TRIM(VictimLastName) != ''
AND VictimFirstMiddle IS NOT NULL
AND TRIM(VictimFirstMiddle) != ''

// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Workflows\BKWorkflow.cs
/*
 * Bankruptcy Flow
 */

using LeadsManagerCORE.Modules;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;
using NLog;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Runtime.CompilerServices;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using AmourgisCOREServices;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Workflows
{
    internal class BKWorkflow : ICommand
    {
        private readonly AMO_Logger logger;
        private readonly AppSettings appSettings;

        public BKWorkflow(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            // Initialize the workflow with the provided app settings
            this.appSettings = appSettings;
            this.logger = logger;
        }

        public async Task ExecuteAsync(string[] args)
        {
            RunAsync();
        }

        public async Task RunAsync(DateTime? date = null, string? downloadDirectory = null)
        {
            
            // Set the date to yesterday
            DateTime processingDate = date ?? DateTime.Now.AddDays(-1);
            string downloadPath = downloadDirectory ?? Path.Combine(appSettings.DownloadDirectory, processingDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"), "Downloaded from SkipTrace");
            // Create the directory if it doesn't exist
            Directory.CreateDirectory(downloadPath);
            SkipTraceHelper _skipTraceHelper = new SkipTraceHelper(appSettings, logger);
            SqlHelper _sqlHelper = new SqlHelper(appSettings, logger);
            LeadDocketHelper _leadDocketHelper = new LeadDocketHelper();
            //MailingHelper _mailingHelper = new MailingHelper();

            try
            {
                // Download SkipTrace results that have an upload date of yesterday
                logger.Info($"Downloading SkipTrace results for {processingDate.ToShortDateString()}...");
                _skipTraceHelper.DownloadSkipTraceResults(processingDate, downloadPath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error downloading SkipTrace results");
                return;
            }

            try
            {
                // Insert the downloaded data into the SQL database
                logger.Info($"Inserting data from {downloadPath} into the database...");
                SqlHelper.InsertDataFromCSV(downloadPath, appSettings);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error inserting data into the database");
                return;
            }

            try
            {
                // Get yesterday's leads from the database and upload them to SkipTrace
                logger.Info($"Uploading leads to SkipTrace for {processingDate.ToShortDateString()}...");
                _skipTraceHelper.UploadLeadsToSkipTrace(processingDate);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error uploading leads to SkipTrace");
                return;
            }

            try
            {
                // Get yesterday's leads from the database and upload them to LeadDocket
                logger.Info($"Uploading leads to LeadDocket for {processingDate.ToShortDateString()}...");
                _leadDocketHelper.UploadLeadsToLeadDocket(processingDate, appSettings);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error uploading leads to LeadDocket");
                return;
            }

            try
            {
                // Get yesterday's leads from the database and send them to Yoder Rapid Mailing
                logger.Info("Sending leads to Yoder Rapid Mailing...");
                //_mailingHelper.SendToYoderRapidMailing(processingDate, appSettings);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error sending leads to Yoder Rapid Mailing");
                return;
            }
        }
    }
}
