// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Workflows\OhioCrashFetch.cs
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Data;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using AmourgisCOREServices;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Modules;
using NLog;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Workflows
{
    internal class OhioCrashFetch : ICommand
    {

        private readonly AMO_Logger logger;
        private readonly AppSettings appSettings;

        public OhioCrashFetch(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            this.appSettings = appSettings;
            this.logger = logger;
        }

        public async Task ExecuteAsync(string[] args)
        {
            logger.Info("OhioCrashFetch started.");
            try
            {
                await RunAsync();
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "An error occurred in OhioCrashFetch.");
                throw;
            }
        }

        public async Task RunAsync()
        {
            string downloadPath = Global.ExcelDownloadPath;

            #region Step 1: Download the Excel sheet from OhioCrash
            logger.Info($"Downloading Excel sheet from {appSettings.OhioCrash.Url} to {downloadPath}");
            Directory.CreateDirectory(downloadPath); // Ensure the download directory exists

            try
            {
                await DownloadExcelSheetFromOhioCrash(appSettings.OhioCrash.Url, downloadPath, appSettings);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error("Error downloading Excel sheet from OhioCrash: " + ex.Message);
                throw;
            }
            #endregion

            #region Step 2: Insert the Excel file into the SQL database
            logger.Info($"Inserting Excel file into SQL database from {downloadPath}");
            try
            {
                await InsertExcelIntoSQLDatabase(downloadPath, appSettings.Sql.ConnectionString, logger);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error inserting Excel file into SQL database");
                throw;
            }
            #endregion

            logger.Info("OhioCrashFetch completed successfully. Ceasing operation in five seconds.");
            Thread.Sleep(5000); // Pause for 5 seconds to allow the database to process the insertions
        }


        private async Task DownloadExcelSheetFromOhioCrash(string url, string downloadPath, AppSettings appSettings)
        {
            // Implementation for downloading the Excel sheet using Selenium
            SkipTraceHelper ohCrash = new SkipTraceHelper(appSettings, logger);
            ohCrash.DownloadExcelSheetFromOhioCrash(url, downloadPath);
        }

        private static async Task InsertExcelIntoSQLDatabase(string excelFilePath, string connectionString, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            // Implementation for inserting only the newest Excel file into SQL database
            SqlHelper sql = new SqlHelper(connectionString, logger);

            var newestFile = Directory.GetFiles(excelFilePath, "*.xlsx")
                .Select(f => new FileInfo(f))
                .OrderByDescending(f => f.LastWriteTime)
                .FirstOrDefault();

            if (newestFile != null)
            {
                logger.Info($"Inserting {newestFile.FullName} into SQL database");
                sql.InsertCrashReportsIntoSqlDatabase(newestFile.FullName);
            }
            else
            {
                logger.Error("No .xlsx files found to insert into SQL database.");
            }

        }
    }
}


// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Workflows\PIRapidMailDispatch.cs
/*
 * PI Workflow
 * Jacob Hayes
 * 30 April 2025
 * 
 * Process: 
 * 1. Navigate to OhioCrash, download an Excel spreadsheet of all the crash reports.
 * 2. Insert the Excel file into the SQL database, checking to ensure we don't insert duplicates.
 * 3. Filter the SQL data to include reports based on our criteria.
 * 4. Generate an Excel spreadsheet and list of filenames for the filtered reports.
 * 5. Save the generated Excel spreadsheet to the Yoder Dropbox.
 * 6. Use the Dropbox API to move the selected PDFs from the Amourgis Dropbox to the Yoder Dropbox.
 * 7. Use the Dropbox API to remove the unselected PDFs from the Amourgis Dropbox.
 */


using LeadsManagerCORE.Modules;
using NLog;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Data;
using System.Linq;
using System.Runtime.CompilerServices;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using AmourgisCOREServices;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Workflows
{
    internal class PIRapidMailDispatch : ICommand
    {

        private readonly AppSettings appSettings;
        private readonly AMO_Logger logger;
        private readonly DropboxHelper dropboxHelper;
        private readonly IOHelper ioHelper;

        public PIRapidMailDispatch(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            this.appSettings = appSettings;
            this.logger = logger;
            this.ioHelper = new IOHelper(appSettings, logger);
            this.dropboxHelper = new DropboxHelper(appSettings, logger);
        }

        public async Task ExecuteAsync(string[] args)
        {
            logger.Info("PIRapidMailDispatch started.");
            try
            {
                await RunAsync();
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "An error occurred in PIRapidMailDispatch.");
                throw;
            }
        }

        public async Task RunAsync()
        {
            string downloadPath = Path.Combine(appSettings.OhioCrash.ExcelDownloadPath, DateTime.Today.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"));
            string excelFilePath = Path.Combine(appSettings.ExcelOutputPath, $"FilteredReports_{DateTime.Now:yyyyMMdd}.xlsx");
            DataTable filteredRecords;
            List<string> pdfFileNames;

            #region now handled via OhioCrashFetch
            //#region Step 1: Download the Excel sheet from OhioCrash
            //logger.Info($"Downloading Excel sheet from {appSettings.OhioCrash.Url} to {downloadPath}");
            //Directory.CreateDirectory(downloadPath); // Ensure the download directory exists

            //try
            //{
            //    await DownloadExcelSheetFromOhioCrash(appSettings.OhioCrash.Url, downloadPath, appSettings);
            //}
            //catch (Exception ex)
            //{
            //    logger.Error("Error downloading Excel sheet from OhioCrash: " + ex.Message);
            //    throw;
            //}
            //#endregion

            //#region Step 2: Insert the Excel file into the SQL database
            //logger.Info($"Inserting Excel file into SQL database from {downloadPath}");
            //try
            //{
            //    await InsertExcelIntoSQLDatabase(downloadPath, appSettings.Sql.ConnectionString);
            //}
            //catch (Exception ex)
            //{
            //    logger.Error(ex, "Error inserting Excel file into SQL database");
            //    throw;
            //}
            //#endregion
            #endregion

            #region Step 3: Filter the SQL data to include reports based on our criteria
            logger.Info($"Filtering SQL data using connection string: {appSettings.Sql.ConnectionString}");
            try
            {
                filteredRecords = await FilterSQLData(appSettings.Sql.ConnectionString, logger);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error filtering SQL data");
                throw;
            }
            #endregion

            // TO DO: Ensure that duplicate filenames AREN'T being added to the list
            #region Step 4: Generate an Excel spreadsheet and list of filenames for the filtered reports
            logger.Info($"Generating Excel spreadsheet for filtered reports in {appSettings.ExcelOutputPath}");

            try
            {
                pdfFileNames = await GenerateExcelSpreadsheetForFilteredReports(filteredRecords, excelFilePath);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error generating Excel spreadsheet for filtered reports");
                throw;
            }
            #endregion

            #region Step 5 and 6: Move the selected PDFs from the Amourgis Dropbox to the Yoder Dropbox, then clean up the Amourgis Dropbox
            logger.Info($"Moving selected PDFs from Amourgis Dropbox to Yoder Dropbox");
            try
            {
                List<string> movedFiles = await MoveSelectedPDFsToYoderDropbox(appSettings, pdfFileNames, appSettings.Dropbox.AmourgisFolder, appSettings.Dropbox.YoderFolder);
                //await MoveSelectedPDFsToYoderDropbox(appSettings, pdfFileNames, appSettings.Dropbox.AmourgisReportFolder, appSettings.Dropbox.YoderFolder);


                logger.Info($"Removing unselected PDFs from Amourgis Dropbox");

                await EmptyAmourgisDropbox(appSettings, appSettings.Dropbox.AmourgisFolder);
                //await EmptyAmourgisDropbox(appSettings, appSettings.Dropbox.AmourgisReportFolder);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.Error(ex, "Error moving or removing PDFs from Amourgis Dropbox");
                throw;
            }
            #endregion
            #region Step 7: Save the generated Excel spreadsheet to the Yoder Dropbox
            finally
            {
                logger.Info($"Saving Excel spreadsheet to Yoder Dropbox at {appSettings.Dropbox.YoderFolder}");
                try
                {
                    await SaveExcelToYoderDropbox(appSettings, excelFilePath, appSettings.Dropbox.YoderFolder);
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    logger.Error(ex, "Error saving Excel spreadsheet to Yoder Dropbox");
                    throw;
                }
            }
            #endregion
        }


        private async Task<DataTable> FilterSQLData(string connectionString, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            // Implementation for filtering SQL data based on criteria
            SqlHelper sql = new SqlHelper(connectionString, logger);
            DataTable filteredRecords = sql.GetFilteredCrashReports();
            return filteredRecords;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Generates an Excel spreadsheet and a list of filenames for the filtered reports.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="records">A DataTable containing all the records to save as an XLSX.</param>
        /// <param name="excelFilePath">The location to save the XLSX file to.</param>
        /// <returns>A list of all the PDF file names that we want to send to Yoder.</returns>
        private async Task<List<string>> GenerateExcelSpreadsheetForFilteredReports(DataTable records, string excelFilePath)
        {

            // Generate the Excel file for Yoder at excelFilePath
            ioHelper.DataTableToExcel(records, excelFilePath);

            // Generate the list of PDF filenames
            List<string> pdfFileNames = new List<string>();
            foreach (DataRow row in records.Rows)
            {
                // get it with an odps_ prefix
                string pdfFileName = $"odps_{row["File Name:"]}";
                pdfFileNames.Add(pdfFileName);

                // get it without the odps_ prefix
                pdfFileName = $"{row["File Name:"]}";
                pdfFileNames.Add(pdfFileName);
            }
            return pdfFileNames.Distinct().ToList();
        }

        private async Task SaveExcelToYoderDropbox(AppSettings appSettings, string excelFilePath, string dropboxPath)
        {
            // Implementation for saving Excel to Yoder Dropbox
            await dropboxHelper.UploadFileAsync(excelFilePath, dropboxPath);
        }

        private async Task<List<string>> MoveSelectedPDFsToYoderDropbox(AppSettings appSettings, List<string> pdfFileNames, string sourceDropboxPath, string destinationDropboxPath)
        {
            // Implementation for moving selected PDFs to Yoder Dropbox
            return await dropboxHelper.MoveFilesAsync(pdfFileNames, sourceDropboxPath, destinationDropboxPath);
        }

        private async Task EmptyAmourgisDropbox(AppSettings appSettings, string dropboxPath)
        {
            // Implementation for removing unselected PDFs from Amourgis Dropbox
            DropboxHelper dropboxHelper = new DropboxHelper(appSettings, logger);
            await dropboxHelper.ClearFolderAsync(dropboxPath);
        }
    }

}


// File: BankruptcyLeadsManager\Workflows\PrintLocalLetters.cs
/* Print Local Letters Process
 * 
 * First, we'll create a local form-filling docx object and fill the form with the data from the SQL database.
 * Then, we'll convert the filled form to a PDF file.
 * We'll also interact with Dropbox to get the Crash Report PDFs.
 * Finally, we'll print the form-filled PDF file, as well as pages 1 and 4 of the Crash Report PDF (duplex) to the local printer.
 */


using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Data;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using AmourgisCOREServices;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Interfaces;
using LeadsManagerCORE.Modules;

namespace LeadsManagerCORE.Workflows
{
    internal class PrintLocalLetters : ICommand
    {
        private readonly AMO_Logger logger;
        private readonly AppSettings appSettings;
        private readonly DropboxHelper dropboxHelper;
        private readonly PrintHelper printHelper;
        private readonly SqlHelper sqlHelper;
        private readonly IOHelper ioHelper;
        public PrintLocalLetters(AppSettings appSettings, AMO_Logger logger)
        {
            this.appSettings = appSettings;
            this.logger = logger;
            this.dropboxHelper = new DropboxHelper(appSettings, logger);
            this.printHelper = new PrintHelper(appSettings, logger);
            this.sqlHelper = new SqlHelper(appSettings, logger);
            this.ioHelper = new IOHelper(appSettings, logger);
        }

        public async Task ExecuteAsync(string[] args)
        {
            logger.LogInformation("PrintLocalLetters started.");
            try
            {
                await RunAsync();
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.LogError(ex, "An error occurred in PrintLocalLetters.");
                throw;
            }
        }

        public async Task RunAsync()
        {
            logger.LogInformation("Starting the print local letters process...");
            string templatePath = appSettings.PILetters.LetterTemplate;
            string outputPath;
            string pdfLetterPath;
            string datedDir = Path.Combine(appSettings.PILetters.OutputPath, DateTime.Today.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"));
            Directory.CreateDirectory(datedDir);
            string printerToUse = appSettings.Printer.ColorPrinter;

            
            try
            {
                // Fill the form with data from the SQL database
                DataTable dtLocalRecords = sqlHelper.GetLocalFilteredCrashReports();

                foreach (DataRow dr in dtLocalRecords.Rows)
                {
                    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(dr["PDFFileName"]?.ToString()))
                    {
                        logger.Warn($"No PDF file name found for ReportID {dr["ReportID"]}");
                        continue;
                    }

                    // Check to see if we have a PDF in Dropbox that matches it with or without the odps_ prefix
                    string originalFileName = dr["PDFFileName"].ToString();
                    string crashReportFileName = $"odps_{originalFileName}";
                    string dropboxPath = $"{appSettings.Dropbox.AmourgisFolder}/{crashReportFileName}";

                    if (!await dropboxHelper.FileExistsInDropboxAsync(dropboxPath))
                    {
                        // Try without the "odps_" prefix
                        crashReportFileName = originalFileName;
                        dropboxPath = $"{appSettings.Dropbox.AmourgisFolder}/{crashReportFileName}";

                        if (!await dropboxHelper.FileExistsInDropboxAsync(dropboxPath))
                        {
                            // Still no PDF? Log a warning and continue, we won't print this one.
                            logger.Warn($"PDF file not found in Dropbox: {dropboxPath}");
                            continue;
                        }
                    }

                    // If we're here, the program has found the file in Dropbox.
                    logger.Info($"Found PDF file in Dropbox: {dropboxPath}");



                    // Set the output path for the filled document
                    outputPath = Path.Combine(datedDir, $"FilledLetter_{dr["ReportID"]}_{dr["VictimLastName"]}_{dr["VictimFirstMiddle"]}.docx");
                    logger.Info($"Attempting to save file to {outputPath} for {dr["VictimFirstMiddle"]} {dr["VictimLastName"]}");
                    // Fill the document's Content Controls with the data from the DataRow
                    printHelper.GenerateFilledDocument(templatePath, outputPath, dr);
                    // Convert the document to a PDF
                    pdfLetterPath = printHelper.ConvertToPdf(outputPath);
                    // Print the filled document to a printer
                    printHelper.PrintPDFDocument(pdfPath: pdfLetterPath, printerName: printerToUse);
                    // Breakpoint here to check the output
                    logger.Info($"Successfully printed document for {dr["VictimFirstMiddle"]} {dr["VictimLastName"]}");


                    // Now, print the Crash Report from Dropbox - but just the first and fourth pages

                    // Download the PDF
                    string localPdfReportPath = Path.Combine(datedDir, crashReportFileName);
                    await dropboxHelper.DownloadFileFromDropboxAsync(dropboxPath, localPdfReportPath);
                    logger.Info($"Downloaded PDF file from Dropbox: {localPdfReportPath}");
                    // Print the first and fourth pages of the PDF
                    printHelper.PrintPDFDocument(pdfPath: localPdfReportPath, printerName: appSettings.Printer.PIPrinter, pages: new[]{1,4});
                    // Breakpoint here to check the output
                    logger.Info($"Printed pages 1 and 4 of the PDF file: {localPdfReportPath}");

                    // Remove the file from Dropbox
                    //await dropboxHelper.DeleteFileFromDropboxAsync(dropboxPath);
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                logger.LogError(ex, "Error in the print local letters process");
            }

            logger.LogInformation("Print local letters process completed.");
        }

    }
}
